)@@G@@CVFLG.           GET TYPE OF VARIABLE TO CONVERT@D@@@J         LOADA A3,QB
)@@G@@KFZERO .         CLEAR OUTPUT AREA  @ @@@J         LOADA A2,DCVSTG .    QC
)@@G@@@D@@@J         LOAD  R1,20,I .           CLEAR 20 WORDS     @^@@@J      QD
)@@G@@   LINK  MO$VEZ . @D@@@J         SETPC 4,DCVSTG .          SET TO WRITE QE
)@@G@@STRING@E@@@J         IF    SDDCBN,ON THEN,CVSTBN . -> BINARY SOURCE     QF
)@@G@@@^@@@J/.       FLOAT DECIMAL  @#@@@JCVFLDC   LABEL .  @E@@@J         LOAQG
)@@G@@DA   X3,DCVFLT .       PLACE WHERE NUMBER IS    @E@@@J         LINK    CQH
)@@G@@VSGPT .          PUT IN THE SIGN IF NEEDED@E@@@J         IF    SDFXFL,OFQI
)@@G@@F THEN,CVFXDC . -> FIXED DECIMAL    @C@@@J         LOADD A7,DCVFLT .    QJ
)@@G@@     GET NUMBER   @E@@@J         IF    A7,NE,0,I THEN,CVSCL0 . -> NON ZEQK
)@@G@@RO NUMBER   @E@@@J         MOVE DCVINT,0,I .         SET EXPONENT TO ZERQL
)@@G@@O     @D@@@J         IF    DCVTST,ZERO THEN,CVRTN . -> NO '.'     @C@@@JQM
)@@G@@         LOAD    A8,'.',I .        GET A '.'    @G@@@J         IF  DCVSTQN
)@@G@@L,NZERO  THEN,CVFLD1 . IN SECOND OR THIRD POSITION?   @D@@@J         STOQO
)@@G@@RE   A8,DCVSTG+FQ2 .   SECOND POSITION    @C@@@J         GOTO  CVSCL9 . QP
)@@G@@           -> FINISH    @#@@@JCVFLD1   LABEL .  @D@@@J         STORE   AQQ
)@@G@@8,DCVSTG+FQ3 .   THIRD POSITION HERE@C@@@J         GOTO  CVSCL9 .       QR
)@@G@@     -> FINISH    @C@@@JCVSCL0   LABEL .                   SCALE NUMBER QS
)@@G@@@B@@@J.        DCVFLT = .C*2**X = C.*2**(X-074)=@A@@@J.        C.*10**(LQT
)@@G@@OG 2 * (X-074) )  @D@@@J         IF    A7,GE,0,I THEN,CVSCL0B . -> + NUMQU
)@@G@@BER   @C@@@J         DLN A7,A7   .       GET ABS(NUMBER)    @ @@@J      QV
)@@G@@   STORED A7,DCVFLT .   @#@@@JCVSCL0B  LABEL .  @D@@@J         LINK CVSCQW
)@@G@@L0A .            CONVERT NUMBER     @D@@@J         GOTO CVSCL9 .        QX
)@@G@@     FINISH OUT THE FORM@ @@@J/.     DIGIT STRING PRODUCER  @F@@@JCVSCL0QY
)@@G@@A  LOCAL .                   USED FOR BOTH FIXED AND FLOAT  @C@@@J      QZ
)@@G@@   SRB   A7,24 .             LEAVE 20XX   @B@@@J         SUB   A7,02074,RA
)@@G@@I .        (X-074)@D@@@J         LOG2Y A7 .                LOG 2 *(X-074RB
)@@G@@)     @E@@@JCVSCL1   LABEL .                   A7=EXPONENT OF 10 NEEDED RC
)@@G@@@ @@@J         LOADD A9,DCVFLT .    @G@@@J         IF    A7,EQ,0,I THEN,RD
)@@G@@CVSCL2 .                 -> NO SCALING    @B@@@J         LOADM A8,A7 .  RE

)@@G@@A3,X  @ @@@ .   A     LMJ   X11,DATAN     @G@@@ .   DATAN AND DATAN2 ARECB
)@@G@@ ENTRY POINTS TO A FUNCTION WHICH COMPUTES THE  @D@@@ .   ARCTANGENT OF CC
)@@G@@ONE OR TWO ARGUMENTS RESPECTIVELY.  @[@@@ .     @A@@@ .   ARGUMENT AND FCD
)@@G@@UNCTION RANGE     @I@@@ .   THE ARGUMENT MUST BE A NORMALIZED, DOUBLE PRCE
)@@G@@ECISION, FLOATING POINT NUMBER.     @H@@@ .   THE FUNCTION RETURNS A NORCF

)@@G@@@[@@@ .     @^@@@ .   FUNCTIONS REFERENCED@]@@@ .   NONE    @[@@@ .     CH
)@@G@@@^@@@ .   ERROR CONDITIONS    @D@@@ .   UNNORMALIZED ARGUMENTS CAUSE ERRCI
)@@G@@OR TERMINATION.   @[@@@ .     @^@@@ .  MATHEMATICAL METHOD  @G@@@ .   IFCJ
)@@G@@ ABS(X) .GE. 4.0, LET Z = 1/X AND ARCTAN(X) = PI/2 - ARCTAN(Z).   @E@@@ CK
)@@G@@.   IF ABS(X) < 0.25, LET Z = X AND ARCTAN(X) = ARCTAN(Z).  @I@@@ .   IFCL
)@@G@@ 0.25 .LE. ABS(X) .LT. 4.0, LET X = TAN(Q + Y), WHERE ABS(TAN(Q)) < 0.25CM
)@@G@@.     @G@@@ .   THEN Z = TAN(Q) = (TAN(Q + Y) - TAN(Y))/(TAN(Q + Y) * TACN
)@@G@@N(Y) + 1)   @F@@@ .   ARCTAN(X) = Q + Y, WHERE Y IS IN A TABLE AND Q = ACO
)@@G@@RCTAN(Z).   @G@@@ .   ARCTAN(Z) IS APPROXIMATED BY A RATIONAL APPROXIMATCP
)@@G@@ION OF THE FORM   @G@@@ .   Z*P(Z**2)/Q(Z**2), WHERE P AND Q ARE 4TH ANDCQ
)@@G@@ 5TH DEGREE POLYNOMIALS @#@@@ .   RESPECTIVELY. @ @@@ .   ARCTAN(-X) = -CR
